things,&nbsp;<em>I</em>&nbsp;<em>know you do</em>–and that’s why&nbsp;<em>I know I’m right</em>… but I think like many people–Heaven is more than just a land of “not evil” as in not evil starvation, because another sign from the Universe made me smile, it said “<strong>good feels good</strong>” and hangs in every Starbucks I see; but so much shit I’ve taken for just that stance, I wonder if we want to go to a Heaven where “<em>good feels boring.</em>”</div> <div> <br /></div> <div style=”text-align: center;”> <a href=”./WHO.html”><img alt=”” border=”0” height=”150” <br /> <div style=”text-align: justify;”> I don’t&nbsp;<span style=’font-family: “comic sans ms” , sans-serif;’>re:<strong>all&gt;</strong>y&lt;</span>&nbsp;<span style=’font-family: “arial black” , sans-serif;’><a href=”./WHO.html” target=”_blank”>care if you hate me</a></span>, though it’s not what I want; if I heard the things i hear in my own mind aloud, I’d probably be hateful too.&nbsp; The sad thing is though, I know they don’t come from me–but from the storm, and for it not stopping,&nbsp;<em>I blame you</em>.&nbsp; See why “Heaven” and see why “sky” and see why these things are our future, and why I see time and sky are nearly the same thing.&nbsp; See&nbsp;<a href=”./2017-06-14-enders-game-prometheus-locke-and.html” target=”_blank”>why</a>&nbsp;“<span style=’font-family: “comic sans ms” , sans-serif;’><a href=”./KEYNES.html” target=”_blank”>seeing I</a></span>” makes all the difference in the world, in this place&nbsp;<span style=’font-family: “arial black” , finally made public, where we finally have a chance to be free–and see I wonder why we keep coming back to do it again?&nbsp; I wonder why we relive years of pain, and years of hunger, and years of everything wrong that we are supposed to set right–I wonder, I really do, if maybe we’re the only grateful generations in all of time thankful to us; because we know what we do.</span><br /> <br /> sans-serif;”>ignorance</i><span style=’font-family: “arial” , “helvetica” , sans-serif;’>&nbsp;is keeping people in&nbsp;<a href=”http://www.docdroid.net/ZkbjdNU/antagonizingpainxe.pdf” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://bit.ly/2hhCj5c&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614087000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEFvJfLgV4CJGgGx7fUUNDxCUYPNw”><img src=”./i.imgur.com/d83V9HR.png” alt=”Inline image 2” width=”323” height=”419” /></a><br /></div><div style=”text-align:center”><center> <div style=”text-align:justify;width:300px”> <h1 id=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-firstHeading” class=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-firstHeading” lang=”en”><font size=”1”>Rat Park&nbsp;</font></h1> <div id=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-bodyContent” class=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-mw-body-content”> <div id=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-mw-content-text” class=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-mw-content-ltr” dir=”ltr” lang=”en”> <div class=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-mw-parser-output”> <div class=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-hatnote m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-navigation-not-searchable”><font size=”1”>For John Calhoun’s rat city, see&nbsp;<a title=”Behavioral sink” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Behavioral_sink” target=”_blank” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Behavioral_sink&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614087000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGhxe_pC6Bu9cNOrj-29-qiEoQh5w”>behavioral sink</a>.</font></div> <p><font size=”1”><strong>Rat Park</strong>&nbsp;was a study into&nbsp;<a class=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-mw-redirect” title=”Drug addiction” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Drug_addiction” target=”_blank” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Drug_addiction&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614087000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFClcDn-VPrfhxMrt0D-tBp_vJovA”>drug addiction</a>&nbsp;conducted in the late 1970s (and published in 1981) by Canadian psychologist&nbsp;<a title=”Bruce K. Alexander” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bruce_K._Alexander” target=”_blank” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bruce_K._Alexander&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614087000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEmP96SswsEkqyP1Y1eARYOwIOJtQ”>Bruce K. Alexander</a>&nbsp;and his colleagues at&nbsp;<a title=”Simon Fraser University” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simon_Fraser_University” target=”_blank” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simon_Fraser_University&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614087000&amp;usg=AFQjCNEVpi8jBTah95ArXoXmRR9_80v8kA”>Simon Fraser University</a>&nbsp;in British Columbia, Canada.</font></p> <p><font size=”1”>Alexander’s hypothesis was that drugs do not cause addiction, and that the apparent addiction to&nbsp;<a title=”Opiate” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Opiate” target=”_blank” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Opiate&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614087000&amp;usg=AFQjCNG-B_zCqytRGUgEPi1_LG7tqqPk3g”>opiate</a>&nbsp;drugs commonly observed in laboratory rats exposed to them is attributable to their living conditions, and not to any addictive property of the drug itself.<sup id=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-cite_ref-Senate_1-0” class=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-reference”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rat_Park#cite_note-Senate-1” target=”_blank” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rat_Park%23cite_note-Senate-1&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614087000&amp;usg=AFQjCNGRehLpWkgoAlyUVi2aJ_2F6UsKpw”>[1]</a></sup></font></p> <p><font size=”1”>To test his hypothesis, Alexander built Rat Park, a large housing colony, 200 times the floor area of a standard laboratory cage. There were 16–20 rats of both sexes in residence, food, balls and wheels for play, and enough space for mating.<sup id=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-cite_ref-Slater_2-0” class=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-reference”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rat_Park#cite_note-Slater-2” target=”_blank” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rat_Park%23cite_note-Slater-2&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614087000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFRioXaRb5prTatPJG8JOkOPV2UUg”>[2]</a></sup>&nbsp;The results of the experiment appeared to support his hypothesis.</font></p> <p><font size=”1”>The two major science journals,&nbsp;<a title=”Science (journal)” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Science_(journal)” target=”_blank” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Science_(journal)&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614087000&amp;usg=AFQjCNH8QqJmEL80f3lS26FTlvy8oECOHg”><em>Science</em></a>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<a title=”Nature (journal)” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nature_(journal)” target=”_blank” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nature_(journal)&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614087000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHm2p5lSxbmDVRr5dwwT4iHbEXEOw”><em>Nature</em></a>, rejected Alexander, Coambs, and Hadaway’s first paper, which appeared instead in&nbsp;<em><a title=”Psychopharmacology (journal)” href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Psychopharmacology_(journal)” target=”_blank” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Psychopharmacology_(journal)&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614087000&amp;usg=AFQjCNFu8GsVoklVohmUVwEQNWNsErwnaQ”>Psychopharmacology</a></em>&nbsp;in 1978. The paper’s publication initially attracted no response.<sup id=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-cite_ref-Alexander1_3-0” class=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-reference”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rat_Park#cite_note-Alexander1-3” target=”_blank” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rat_Park%23cite_note-Alexander1-3&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614087000&amp;usg=AFQjCNG17Sd-PGMU-MxIKz_xfczTrS6Ffg”>[3]</a></sup>&nbsp;Within a few years, Simon Fraser University withdrew Rat Park’s funding.<sup id=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-cite_ref-4” class=”m_2987020573415560067m_5879822677986557550m_730192481514457090gmail-m_-4059995067227275298gmail-reference”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rat_Park#cite_note-4” target=”_blank” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rat_Park%23cite_note-4&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614087000&amp;usg=AFQjCNF3dDzUTZPkyEl3zf-E_Zot861BeA”>[4]</a></sup></font></p> <blockquote> <p style=”text-align:center”></p><aasdf href=”http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=sENM2wA_FTg” > <a href=”http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IXPOHCsgWFw”> <img src=”./i.imgur.com/UJ2Xjem.png” alt=”Inline image 4” width=”293” height=”180” style=”margin-right:0px” /></a> <br/> <div> <div><strong>”Look,&nbsp;<a href=”./DICKCLARK.html” rel=”noopener” target=”_blank” data-saferedirecturl=”http://www.google.com/url?hl=en&amp;q=http://bit.ly/2i966yS&amp;source=gmail&amp;ust=1535597614088000&amp;usg=AFQjCNHC7gIfkTk_14MsALEJOxve2myD3A”>he is coming with the clouds,” and “every eye will see him, even those who pierced him”; and all peoples on earth “will mourn</a>&nbsp;because of him.” So shall it be!
